NPC1.Name = "NPC 1"
NPC1.Parent = autoframNPC
NPC1.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
NPC1.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.258762002, 0)
NPC1.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 50)
NPC1.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
NPC1.Text = "Tomura"
NPC1.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
NPC1.TextSize = 14.000
NPC1.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
	if game.PlaceId == 1499868983 then

		game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(1499872953,game.Players.LocalPlayer)
	end
	if not game:IsLoaded() then
		local loadedcheck = Instance.new("Message",workspace)
		loadedcheck.Text = 'Loading...'
		game.Loaded:Wait()
		loadedcheck:Destroy()
	end
	game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:ChangeState(0)
	tweenService, tweenInfo = game:GetService("TweenService"), TweenInfo.new(0, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
	tween = tweenService:Create(game:GetService("Players")["LocalPlayer"].Character.HumanoidRootPart, tweenInfo, {CFrame = CFrame.new(-94.31147, 1909.06897, 189.325989, -0.600140691, -0.347291946, 0.720568895, -2.98023188e-08, 0.900829911, 0.434172183, -0.799894452, 0.260564357, -0.540624678)})
	tween:Play()
	wait(2)
	game.Players.bot1_100.Character.Head.Anchored = true
	game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart:Destroy();

	while wait() do
		pcall(function()
			skills = true
			keytospam1 = "Q"
			keytospam2 = "Z"
			keytospam3 = "X"
			keytospam4 = "C"
			keytospam5 = "V"
			keytospam6 = "B"
			local LP = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
			local VIM = game:GetService("VirtualInputManager")
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam1], false, game)
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam2], false, game)
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam3], false, game)
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam4], false, game)
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam5], false, game)
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam6], false, game)
		end)
	end

end)

NPC2.Name = "NPC 2"

NPC2.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
	-- auto fram Noumu
	if game.PlaceId == 1499868983 then

		game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(1499872953,game.Players.LocalPlayer)
	end
	if not game:IsLoaded() then
		local loadedcheck = Instance.new("Message",workspace)
		loadedcheck.Text = 'Loading...'
		game.Loaded:Wait()
		loadedcheck:Destroy()
	end
	skills = true
	keytospam1 = "F"
	local LP = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
	local VIM = game:GetService("VirtualInputManager")
	VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam1], false, game)
	wait(2)
	game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:ChangeState(0)
	tweenService, tweenInfo = game:GetService("TweenService"), TweenInfo.new(0, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear)
	tween = tweenService:Create(game:GetService("Players")["LocalPlayer"].Character.HumanoidRootPart, tweenInfo, {CFrame = CFrame.new(256.290009, 1897.68066, 796.912231, -0.113724999, 0.00327029359, 0.993506908, -2.9103827e-11, 0.999994636, -0.00329164881, -0.993512273, -0.000374342781, -0.113724396)})
	tween:Play()
	wait(2)
	game.Players.bot1_100.Character.Head.Anchored = true
	game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart:Destroy();

	while wait() do
		pcall(function()
			skills = true
			keytospam1 = "Q"
			keytospam2 = "Z"
			keytospam3 = "X"
			keytospam4 = "C"
			keytospam5 = "V"
			keytospam6 = "B"
			local LP = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
			local VIM = game:GetService("VirtualInputManager")
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam1], false, game)
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam2], false, game)
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam3], false, game)
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam4], false, game)
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam5], false, game)
			VIM:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode[keytospam6], false, game)
		end)
	end
end)

login.Name = "login"
login.Parent = GUI_login
login.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
login.Size = UDim2.new(0, 417, 0, 33)
login.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
login.Text = "login"
login.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
login.TextSize = 14.000
login.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
	if username.Text == '1' and password.Text == '1' then
		GUI_login.Visible = false
		bot1_100.Visible = true
		game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore(
		"SendNotification",
		{
			Title = "Login Success";
			Text = "By z_z"
		}
		)game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore(
		"SendNotification",
		{
			Title = "Login Success";
			Text = "By z_z"
		}
		)
		local mt = getrawmetatable(game)
		local nm = mt.__namecall
		setreadonly(mt,false)
		mt.__namecall = newcclosure(function(self,...)
			if getnamecallmethod() == 'Kick' or getnamecallmethod() == 'kick' then
				game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(game.PlaceId)
			end

			return nm(self,...)
		end)
		local VirtualUser=game:service'VirtualUser'
		game:service'Players'.LocalPlayer.Idled:connect(function()
			VirtualUser:CaptureController()
			VirtualUser:ClickButton2(Vector2.new())
		end)

		local hint = Instance.new("Hint",game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui)
		hint.Text = "start anti afk"
		hint.Name = game.JobId
		wait(1)
		hint:Destroy()
		db = false
		mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse()

		mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)
			if key:lower() == "," then
				if db == false then
					db = true
					local ts = game:GetService("TeleportService")

					local p = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer



					ts:Teleport(game.PlaceId, p)
				else
					db = false
					--code for exit
				end
			end
		end)

	end
end)

local function VOBPRPG_fake_script() -- exit.LocalScript 
	local script = Instance.new('LocalScript', exit)

	script.Parent.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		script.Parent.Parent.Visible = false
	end)




end
coroutine.wrap(VOBPRPG_fake_script)()
local function UNXGXYQ_fake_script() -- opengui.LocalScript 
	local script = Instance.new('LocalScript', opengui)

	local frame = script.Parent.Parent.bot1_100  -- change “Test” to the name of the frane
	local open = false

	script.Parent.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
		if frame.Visible == false then
			frame.Visible = true
		end
	end)

end
coroutine.wrap(UNXGXYQ_fake_script)()

   for i,v in pairs(workspace.NPCs:GetChildren()) do
if string.find(v.Name, "") and v:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and v.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
